***находить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:находить.html>находи́ть</a> (1303)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:находить.html>находи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naxodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>найти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to find</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to think, to consider</li>
<li>to come across</li>
<li>to happen to have</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:находить.html>находи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naxodítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to find</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:находиться.html>нахо́диться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naxóditʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:найтись.html>найти́сь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be found, to turn up</li>
<li>to be located, to be situated <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">no perfective form</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to be in some condition <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">no perfective form</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:находиться.html>находи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:распутье.html>распу́тье</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>naxodítʹsja</b> na raspútʹje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be in a crossroad</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to happen to have, to be found, to be discovered
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:найтись.html>найти́сь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">najtísʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:находить.html>находи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naxodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to repletion, to satiation, to the full</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to walk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:находиться.html>находи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naxodítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">no imperfective form</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to walk for a long time</li>
<li>to tire oneself by walking</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>хо<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ди́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-наход-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ход.html>хо́д</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:выя.html>вы́й</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нахохлиться.html>нахо́хлиться</a> (18066)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">хохлить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xoxlitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нахохлиться.html>нахо́хлиться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naxóxlitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нахо́хливаться</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">хо́хлиться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to ruffle up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to look morose or sullen</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>хо́х<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>лить</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — нахохливаться, хохлиться.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нацарапать.html>нацара́пать</a> (22921)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царапать.html>цара́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">carápatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нация.html>на́ция</a> (2873)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">natio</i>.
</p>

***начало.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>начало</a> (998)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">начѧло</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">načęlo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*načędlo</i>. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>нача́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">načátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ло</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ken-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">new, fresh</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">recent</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ceno-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>нача́ло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">načálo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>нача́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>нача́ла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>нача́л</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>beginning, commencement, onset, start
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:начало.html>нача́ле</a></b> 80-х <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>годо́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>načále</b> 80-x godóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in the early 1980s</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>source, origin</li>
<li><i>(plural)</i> principles, basis, basics</li>
<li>command, authority</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:основа.html>осно́ва</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">osnóva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>на́чало</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">náčalo</span>)

***начать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>нача́ть</a> (147)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*načęti</i>, also see <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">начѧти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">načęti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-чать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-čatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ken-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">new, fresh</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">recent</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ceno-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>нача́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">načátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начинать.html>начина́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to begin, to start, to commence</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начальный.html>нача́льный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">načálʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ча́ть</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:начаться.html>нача́ться</a> (543)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>нача́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">načátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начаться.html>нача́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">načátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начинаться.html>начина́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to begin, to start, to set in, to break out</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>нача́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">načátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Colloquial pronunciation often puts the stress on the prefix in the past masculine, neuter, and plural, i.e. <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начаться.html>на́чался</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:начаться.html>на́чалось</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:начаться.html>на́чались</a></span>, or on the stem in the past masculine, i.e. <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начаться.html>нача́лся</a></span>.</li></ul>
